


Camera mount STL file and Fusion file has been provided in the camera_mount_CAD_files directory. 

Additionally [this tripod screw](https://www.amazon.com/dp/B0BL3DV6PW?ref=ppx_pop_mob_ap_share&th=1) was purchased to allow mounting using universal screw point. 
One issue we did face with the screw was that it was too long, so we recommend measuring the model again and making sure it does not max out the hole depth.

## Preview of the STL Model
[cad_model](<camera_mount_CAD_files/Camera_Mount_ascii.stl>)
